Important News

Memorial Week for the Central Government and the National Government

▲Central Party Headquarters: At 9:00 AM on the 14th, the Central Party Headquarters held the 55th Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Central Committee members Chen Guofu, Wang Zhengting, and Enhe Batu, along with guests Sun Zhen and She Tonghua, representatives of the Ningbo City Yin County Boy Scout Troop from Zhejiang, and 400-500 staff members from the Central Party Headquarters, attended. Chairman Chen Guofu presided over the ceremony. Afterwards, Wang Zhengting delivered a report, stating that when considering our nation's position, the rebellion of Yan Xishan and his reactionary elements has a significant impact. Whether our country can be unified and whether we can implement sovereign power hinges on this. Because a nation's strength lies in its sovereign power. Now, Yan Xishan and others are acting recklessly and rebelliously, which is destroying sovereign power and undermining the foundation of the Chinese nation, turning it into a separatist situation. If a country becomes a separatist form, it will be impossible to gain equal status internationally. Therefore, the current actions of Yan Xishan and others pose a danger of putting the Chinese nation to death. If we do not use all our strength to eliminate them, we will not be able to seek our own survival. As for the methods of suppressing the rebellion, the central government is of course prepared. Now, we only need to consider what fundamental methods to use to gradually make our country sound and to make our country's power grow stronger. Of course, construction is still the foundation. I believe that the goal of construction should be to increase the happiness of ordinary people in general, increase the abilities of ordinary people in general, and enable ordinary people to be happy. There are three ways to achieve this goal: (1) Facilitate transportation to increase production capacity, so we must immediately implement road repairs and river dredging. (2) Increase the common knowledge of ordinary people in general, which is to implement universal education, and be sure to enable those engaged in a certain industry to have specialized knowledge and skills in their own industry. For example, China has been an agricultural country since ancient times, but its agricultural production volume is far behind that of the United States. American farmers have sufficient common knowledge and considerable specialized knowledge and skills in agriculture. Therefore, the cotton acreage planted in China and the United States is equal, but the cotton production in the United States often exceeds our cotton production by three or four times. By analogy, we can see that the success of construction cannot begin without universal education. (3) Promote national sports. We must know that we must first have a strong body to have a strong spirit. With a strong spirit, we will have a strong career. Therefore, the health of a country's people often affects the strength or weakness of the nation. Therefore, from the fundamental point of view of construction, we must first work hard on the above three points, and then the success of construction will be easier, and it will be easier to gain equal status internationally. The meeting adjourned after the report. ▲National Government: At 10:00 AM on the same day, the National Government held Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Chiang Kai-shek, Tan Yankai, Sun Ke, Zhu Peide, Gu Yingfen, Shao Yuanchong, Yi Peiji, Chen Yi, Wei Daoming, Zhang Nanxian, Jiang Menglin, Liu Ruihuan, Zhou Yawei, Li Jinlun, Zhang Wohua, and more than 300 officials and military personnel attended. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek presided over the ceremony. Afterwards, Secretary Qian Changzhao made the following political report: (1) The Five-Power Naval Conference has been open for a long time. The several difficulties of the conference have been explained in detail before the conference opened. Now, the difficulties have not been resolved, but the lack of sincerity of the countries' infighting has been clearly exposed. The situation of the conference in the past few weeks was dangerous and there was a possibility of breakdown. Later, the Japanese government accepted the US proposal on the tonnage of cruisers and submarines. Although some reservations were attached, the atmosphere among the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan has eased a lot. The agreement among the three countries can already be established. Some people say that Japan has been forced to negotiate unsuccessfully. The brothers believe that this is still Japan's cleverness. At this conference, the United Kingdom and the United States are at the center. These two countries have always been the most face-saving. If the conference completely fails, it will be very stimulating for Japan, France, and Italy. The combination of the United Kingdom and the United States will inevitably become more consolidated. France and Italy have more interests in the mainland. Japan is a maritime country and will inevitably be restrained everywhere in the future. Its acceptance of the US proposal is to befriend the United Kingdom and leave room for future maritime activities. The Japanese government can bend and stretch, which can be seen from this. According to the current situation, the naval conference will never completely fail, and the expression of the British and American authorities is very positive. As for France and Italy, they have never been willing to give in. On the one hand, because they do not have to compromise with the United Kingdom and the United States for the time being, on the other hand, because the United Kingdom and the United States may not pay much attention to their compromises. Whether the result is a five-power agreement or only a three-power agreement depends on the contact in the next few days. (2) Ge Feng does not know the people and does not know the country. Their elimination is of course very fast. What the central government is worried about now is not the war but the people. Years of natural and man-made disasters have exhausted their vitality. This time, Ge Feng's rebellion will directly and indirectly affect the people. Before the central government puts down the rebellion, the people will have to endure the pain temporarily in a short period of time. When the feudal warlords are destroyed, the central government can concentrate on construction, and the people's vitality can be gradually restored. As for the anti-rebellion army, it should always have the heart to love the people and do things to defend the people. This point has been described in detail in Jiang's book, and after the overall situation is settled, the only most important task of the central government is to reduce the burden and pain of the people. (3) The National Games closed the day before yesterday. The spirit of this conference was very good and the results were considerable. However, looking around our nation, it is still sluggish. Ordinary people generally have insufficient energy in their youth. Before the age of fifty, they have signs of aging. Most of them retire after the age of sixty, which is really ashamed compared to European and American countries. A few days ago, an American newspaper published the ages and photos of the judges of the US Supreme Court. The oldest one was eighty-nine years old and the youngest one was fifty-eight years old, and they were all energetic and showed no signs of aging. It is really admirable. Now, if our nation wants to cheer up, the first thing to do is to exercise our physique. Exercising our physique must be universal and persistent. Since the first Far East Games, there have been two shortcomings in exercising our physique. One is that it is not universal. Sports are almost limited to the academic community. The industrial and commercial circles rarely join. The reason is that the industrial and commercial circles are not very interested in sports, and there are no facilities in the society to give them opportunities to practice. One is that it is not persistent. It is often sporadic, so progress is not seen. In recent years, we have repeatedly lagged behind in competitions with Japan and the Philippines. The reason is that the athletes themselves do not work hard, and at the same time, the society is gradually indifferent to the Games. The above two shortcomings must be remedied. This matter is greatly related to the promotion of the nation. In addition to exercising our physique, sports can also cultivate a spirit of fair competition and integrity. A true athlete not only has skills, but also has self-cultivation. If this kind of self-cultivation is moved to the society, it can also create a very good atmosphere. Sports are so important. For the sake of promotion, the government has decided to hold the National Games in the capital next year. The budget is 500,000 yuan, and Lin Sen, Zhu Peide, He Yingqin, Wu Tiecheng, and Wei Daoming have been designated as members of the preparatory committee. (4) The German Industrial Inspection Group is coming to Beijing soon. The group has a total of eight people and is the representative of the German industrial circle. They are very knowledgeable and experienced in various industries. Two of them are very clear about the situation in our country. They are coming here with sincerity. It is not like ordinary inspection groups who attend several banquets and say a few irrelevant words and then leave. Since they are sincere, we should especially welcome them and have three hopes. Before their inspection, we are very willing to listen to their experiences of fighting hard in difficulties and hardships with the spirit of perseverance and fortitude in the past ten years, because that kind of spirit is worthy of emulation, and that kind of experience can be our model. This is the first hope. When they are inspecting, we are more willing to listen to their criticisms, as much as possible. We must know that all industries in our country are immature. Because they are immature, we should be more cautious during the period of laying the foundation. If we go down the wrong road, it is often a tiny mistake that leads to great errors. Therefore, if they criticize as much as possible at this moment, it is of great importance to the future of our country's industry. This is the second hope. After they inspect and return to Germany, they will definitely be more clear about the situation of our country's industry and more understanding of our country's government and people. In the future, if there is an opportunity, the two countries can seek mutual assistance on a completely equal footing. This is the third hope. With their sincerity this time, they will never disappoint us. At the same time, we should give them all kinds of convenience and opportunities to inspect and negotiate.

Important News 2

86th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Committee

On the 14th, the 86th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Committee was attended by Hu Hanmin, Tan Yankai, Guo Fu, and Sun Ke, with Li Wenfan and others present as observers. Chairman Tan Yankai. The resolutions are as follows: (1) Article 8 of the Provincial Representative Assembly Election Law was revised to: "If the location of the district branch is too far away, or if there are other difficulties, and it is not possible to convene a primary election representative assembly, the county (city) party headquarters or the special provincial-level party headquarters may decide to adopt a postal election method to elect representatives to attend the Provincial Representative Assembly." Article 10 was revised to: "After electing representatives to attend the Provincial Representative Assembly, each county (city) party headquarters or special provincial-level party headquarters shall report the election situation, together with the election ballots, list of representatives, registered list of party members after the registration is completed, etc., to the provincial party headquarters, and issue certificates of election." (2) Approved the organizational rules of the Central Committee for the Review of Party Members' Applications for Further Studies. (3) Approved the revised draft of the party fee collection regulations. (4) The Central Supervisory Committee sent 17 cases of disciplinary actions against party members. Those permanently expelled from the party include Wu Qian, Chen Junyu, Yu Qiqin, Xie Wei (Zhejiang Xuanping), Guan Bingxiang (Jin Hedong City), and Tang Shaozhang (Zhejiang Fenshui), six people. Those expelled from the party include Zhou Lianqing (Xiang Xiangxiang), Feng Dengyun, Feng Guojun, Yuan Zonghai, Feng Buyun, Huo Weib, (Ji Anguo County), Shao Bingsheng (Shanghai), Chen Junai (Xiang Xiangtan), Hu Ronghua (Jin Qinyuan), Deng Liangchun (Hunan), and Qiao Rongke (Yu Xinyang), eleven people. Those expelled from the party for three years include Chen Juexian, one person (Su Songjiang). Those expelled from the party for two years include Zhou Huang and Zhao Jixing, two people (Zhe Zhuji). Those expelled from the party for one year include Yin Zhulin, Hai Jiang, and Bian Yudong, two people (Su Funing). All were resolved to be handled accordingly.

Resolution of the Changes in Yan Zhongru's Department

▲ The reason is that the Li Regiment opposes Yan Zhongru.

▲ He Jian formulates four solutions.

Changsha Correspondence: Li Xuan of the First Regiment of the Independent Fifth Brigade, Yan Zhongru's Department, had a disturbance in Baoqing, cut off the Changbao telephone line, and cut off transportation. For a while, the situation between Changsha and Baoqing was tense. He Jian initially attached great importance to it and ordered the Changtan armies to be on strict alert. On one hand, he sent personnel to investigate the truth. Later, on the 19th, he received a telegram from Li Xuan, clearly stating that this action was to oppose Brigadier General Yan Zhongru personally and absolutely support the Commander-in-Chief (referring to He Jian). At the same time, he also asked his brother Li Zemin to come to the province to present the situation to He Jian and requested that the Li Regiment be separated from the Yan Brigade and reorganized into other troops. Only then did He Jian know that the disturbance in the Li Regiment was not as serious as the rumors outside. He immediately convened the military officers in the province and Yan Zhongru and others to discuss the handling methods. It was generally agreed that soldiers who acted freely and opposed officials were inappropriate. However, at this time of turmoil, in order to avoid the expansion of the matter, they had to temporarily approve the request and decided on a solution: (1) The Li Xuan Regiment will be reorganized into the 15th Division directly under He Jian, and the Wang Xianyi Supplement Regiment of the 15th Division will be incorporated into the Independent Fifth Brigade. (2) Li Zemin, Deputy Brigadier General of the Independent Fifth Brigade, can no longer cooperate with Yan. Cancel the title of Deputy Brigadier General and transfer him to be an advisor to the Fourth Route Army Headquarters. (3) The Li Xuan Regiment disbanded the special service battalion guns under the Yan Brigade in Baoqing and returned them to the Yan Brigade. The General Headquarters will find ways to supplement the guns insufficient for the Wang (Xianyi) Regiment. (4) The Yan Brigade's original Wan (Fangzhi) Regiment and the newly incorporated Wang (Xianyi) Regiment moved to Liuli to suppress bandits. The Li Xuan Regiment will still be stationed in Baoqing for reorganization and training. The above methods were satisfactory to both Yan Zhongru and Li Xuan. The situation in Changbao was resolved from then on. The telegram resumed on the 11th, and the Changbao car route continued to operate as usual. According to people from Baoqing, the order in Baoqing is as usual. Except for the sound of guns discovered on the evening of the 7th when the special service battalion guns were handed over, although people were very frightened afterwards, fortunately there was no disturbance. (April 12)

Guangdong Army Defeats Communist Bandits in Beijiang

▲ The Communist bandits' collection of military supplies in Nanxiong and their invasion of Renshi.

▲ The six regiments of the Guangdong Army entered Shao to suppress and recovered Shixing on the 7th.

Guangzhou Correspondence: After the two Communist bandit forces, Peng Dehuai and Zhu De, entered and occupied Nanshi and Renhua, their purpose was to collect money and live the lives of bandits. Therefore, after arriving in Nanxiong, they used the name of Wei De to extort 100,000 yuan in military supplies from the Nanxiong Chamber of Commerce, limiting the payment to three days. The military supplies were collected by each store according to their household. The distribution method was divided into five grades: The first grade is silver shops, shipping agents, foreign goods companies, pawnshops, eight or nine businesses, etc., each household should pay 3,000 yuan. The second grade is silk and satin cloth foreign goods stores, each household should pay 2,000 yuan. The third grade is miscellaneous stores, each household should pay 1,500 yuan. The fourth grade is local goods merchants, each household should pay 1,000 yuan. The fifth grade is handicraft stores and small merchants, each household should pay 500 yuan. When the Communist bandits did not arrive in Nanxiong, the local wealthy had already moved away. The middle class who were unfortunate were forced to close down many of their shops due to this extortion. As soon as the Communist bandits arrived in Nanxiong, they first burned down the county party headquarters and searched for party headquarters personnel and many county government officials. It is heard that more than ten people were killed. Nanxiong County Magistrate Mei Yiqiang fled to Shao in advance and was spared. The Communist bandits also paid attention to propaganda. After the mail was checked, the back of the letters was covered with various slogans, no less than a hundred characters, all in red. On the day of the fall of Xionghou, Zhu De sent a bandit force to plunder Renhua. Therefore, in the afternoon of the third day, Renhua and Shixing were successively captured by the bandits. This is the story of the Communist bandits' ravaging the Xionghou area. At that time, the defense troops were weak and the bandit forces were vast, so the government army was forced to retreat and wait for reinforcements. In recent days, the provinces of Wu and Wu have sent large troops to concentrate in Shaoguan, including the Peng Linsheng Regiment of the 59th Division, the Wu Wenxian Regiment of the 63rd Division, the Chen Hanguang Department of the Headquarters Guard Regiment, and the Zeng Youren Department of the Third Independent Regiment. Recently, the Zhang Zhiying Department of the Fourth Independent Regiment was also transferred north. The Zhang Regiment took the Fu'an ship on the 6th and returned to the provincial capital from the Haikoubu of the South Road, and transferred to the Yuehan car to Shao. The Eighth Route Army Headquarters appointed Wu Wenxian as the Commander of the Beijiang Bandit Suppression. Wu has selected the former North District Post-Disaster Public Office in Shao as the Beijiang Bandit Suppression Headquarters, preparing to lead the Beijiang armies to suppress the Zhu Peng Communist bandits. After the regiments concentrated in Shaoguan, Wu immediately held a bandit suppression conference in Shao. The regiments then set off in separate ways. It is estimated that the Wu Xian Zeng Youren Departments concentrated in Jilongxu, 95 miles above Shao, to block the Communist bandits in Shixing from going south. The Chen Hanguang Peng Linsheng Regiments concentrated in Zhoutian, 85 miles above Shao, to control the Communist bandits in Renhua from rushing out. The road from Jilongxu to Shixing is commanded by Wu Wenxian, and the road from Zhoutian to Renhua is commanded by Chen Hanguang, with Zhang Zhiying as the reserve tunnel, and thousands of local militias from Qujiang, Renhua, and Shixing are gathered to cooperate in attacking in separate ways. Shao City is maintained by the Yi Wenwei Department of the 9th Gendarmerie Team. Recent news from the front, on the 5th, the road from Jilonghao to attack Shixing has begun to contact the Communist bandits in Jiangkou (Jiangkou is 20 miles away from Shixing). After a fierce battle until noon on the 6th, Chen Hanguang drew a battalion to help. The Communist bandits could not support it, and the 100,000 yuan extorted by the Communist bandits in Nanxiong had arrived, and they had no intention to fight. They withdrew from Shixing on the 7th. However, the authorities were afraid that they would defect to the Dongjiang River, and have telegraphed the Mao Weishou Brigade stationed in the upper reaches of the Dongjiang River to quickly send tunnels to Lianping to intercept. At the same time, the Jin Handing Division of Southern Jiangxi was telegraphed to order the Tang Brigade Yang Yingzhi Regiment and the Zhang Brigade Xiao Xixian Regiment to go south to encircle the Communist bandits behind Nanxiong, so as to encircle and annihilate the Communist bandits in the short term. (April 9)

Northeast Infantry, Artillery and Air Force Grand Exercise

▲ Live ammunition shooting is performed.

Shenyang Correspondence: The Northeast Infantry, Artillery and Air Force joint exercise began on the 1st of this month along the Hun River. In order to enable the exercise personnel to experience the real situation of the battlefield and understand the coordinated actions of the various units during the attack, Commander Zhang Xueliang and Deputy Commander Wang Yizhe of the Commander's Headquarters specially conducted live ammunition shooting at the Beidaying shooting range at 10:00 am on the 10th (originally scheduled for the 8th due to wind and snow). On that day, the gale was like a roar, but the guests who came to visit were still very enthusiastic. In addition to military, political, academic, and business dignitaries, Fang Benren, the central representative stationed in Shenyang, and Men Zhizhong, the representative of Feng Yuxiang, also arrived on time. Students who went to visit included Tongze and Peiying schools. A shed was set up facing north in the field, with two scissor-shaped binoculars on it. In front of the shed, trenches crisscrossed and three groups of artillery cover bodies were set up. After Zhang Xueliang arrived at the scene, Deputy Commander (First Brigade Commander) Wang Yizhe of the Commander's Headquarters saluted and reported, and immediately sounded the signal to issue orders. For a time, the messenger soldiers wearing green disguises ran back and forth, and the officers and soldiers in the trenches issued orders to measure and write reports. Senior officials and guests held binoculars to watch, and the situation was extremely busy. Twelve large mountain guns were lined up in the field. In the yellow sand, the cannons roared, and the smoke and dust rose in the distance where the shells landed, giving the impression of being on the battlefield. The exercise did not end until 3:00 pm. In this exercise, the infantry research class students of the First Brigade were the infantry exercise commanders, the First Brigade infantry research class soldiers' team and the First Brigade headquarters troops were the exercise troops, the artillery research class students of the Jiangwutang were the artillery exercise commanders, the artillery research class teaching team was the exercise troops, the aviation research class students of the Jiangwutang were the aviation exercise commanders, the aviation research class guidance team was the exercise troops, the engineering research class students of the Jiangwutang were the engineering exercise commanders, and the engineering research class teaching team was the engineering exercise troops. The sound of rumbling on that day was quite clear even in the city. (April 11)

Details of the Kunshan Military Police Crushing Lake Bandits at Yangcheng Lake

Suzhou Correspondence: On the 12th of this month, the 1st Battalion of the 28th Regiment stationed in Kunshan, together with the 12th Water Public Security Team, fiercely suppressed lake bandits at Lianhua Dou in Yangcheng Lake. Afterwards, scattered bandits were intercepted in various lakeside areas. At the same time, the military and police are still continuing to search for and suppress the remaining bandits. The detailed situation is recorded as follows:

▲Names of Rescued Hostages In the battle of Lianhua Dou, a total of thirty-four hostages were rescued by the government troops. The names, ages, and origins are as follows: Zhu Jinshan (28 years old, Jinshan native, rice merchant, residing in Zhangyan), Zhu Guangxian (26 years old, Jinshan native, rice merchant, residing in Zhangyan), Zhu Yinxiang (18 years old, Jinshan native, rice merchant, residing in Zhangyan), Tao Guokang (15 years old, Jinshan native, student, residing in Zhangyan), Ling Xianyu (24 years old, Shandong native), Huang Houchu (27 years old, Jinshan native, school principal, residing in Zhangyan), Zhang Zhaochang (21 years old, Jinshan native, teacher, residing in Zhangyan), Gu Shijie (12 years old, Jinshan native, student, residing in Zhangyan), Zhang Shouyi (13 years old, Jinshan native, student, residing in Zhangyan), Wu Lejun (14 years old, Jinshan native, student, residing in Zhangyan), Xi Chengyuan (13 years old, Jinshan native, student, residing in Zhangyan), Xu Songyu (27 years old, Jinshan native, Zhenshen Company, residing in Zhangpu), Wen Xingqiao (41 years old, Jinshan native, manager of Zhenshen Company, residing in Zhangpu), Chen Yizhang (20 years old, Jinshan native, merchant, residing in Zhangyan), Xia Shijie (10 years old, Jinshan native, student, residing in Zhangyan), Jiang Juanqing (35 years old, Jinshan native, porcelain business, residing in Zhangyan), Fan Qirui (56 years old, Jinshan native, clothing store, residing in Zhangyan), Li Xinglin (53 years old, Jinshan native, pawnshop, residing in Zhangyan), Wang Yongtai (29 years old, Yangzhou native, water police), Wu Aying (12 years old, Kunshan native, farmer, residing in Qingyang Port), Guo Geting (55 years old, Jinshan native, farmer, residing in Qingyang Port), Sun Anan (8 years old, Jinshan native, residing in Zhangyan), Guo Zhangshi (37 years old, Jinshan native, farmer, residing in Zhangyan), Guo Linsheng (14 years old, Jinshan native, farmer, residing in Zhangyan), Pan Xushi (45 years old, Jinshan native, foreign goods, residing in Zhangyan), Xia Wushi (40 years old, Jinshan native, residing in Zhangyan), Xia Wushi's daughter (8 years old, Jinshan native, residing in Zhangyan), Shen Wushi (43 years old, Jinshan native, foreign goods, residing in Zhangyan), Shen Jingying (Shen Wushi's eldest daughter, 14 years old, Jinshan native, residing in Zhangyan), Shen Jingfang (Shen Wushi's youngest daughter, 10 years old, Jinshan native, residing in Zhangyan), Yan Jiesheng (51 years old, Jinshan native, pawnshop, residing in Zhangyan), Wang Jieqi (34 years old, Jinshan native, pawnshop, residing in Zhangyan), Zhao Citing (15 years old, Jinshan native, student, residing in Zhangyan), Zhang Siming (16 years old, Jinshan native, student, residing in Zhangyan), Huang Weijing (16 years old, Jinshan native, student, residing in Zhangyan). The above hostages have now been handed over by the regimental headquarters to the Kunshan First District Office, awaiting their families to claim them.

▲Circumstances of the Firefight On the 12th of this month, after the Kunshan Camp Commander Kuang learned of the discovery of a large gang of lake bandits at Xia Xiongtian (i.e., Xia Xintian), he personally led two infantry companies and one machine gun company, together with nine police boats from the 12th Water Police Team, and set off towards Yangcheng Lake. Later, upon reaching Bacheng, considering it to be a vital waterway to Taicang, Captain Li led three police boats to stay in Bacheng to guard the area. The remaining six police boats followed Commander Kuang forward and indeed found hundreds of bandits at Xia Xiongtian, whereupon they opened fire. At that time, the lake bandits were on the west side, and the military police were on the east side. The government troops then used machine guns to strafe them. After an hour, the bandits began to collapse and fled towards Lianhua Dou in the rear. The military police pursued closely. The bandits fought and fled. When they reached Lianhua Dou (this place borders Yangcheng Village, separated by about three miles of water, belonging to Wuxian County, about eighteen miles from Bacheng), the bandits, seeing that they could not escape by water in the rear, turned around and pounced on the military police. However, the bandits' bullets were exhausted, and they stubbornly resisted in hand-to-hand combat, eventually using their gun barrels to strike at the military police. The military police then fixed bayonets onto their rifles and stabbed at the bandits. At that time, some bandits jumped into the water and drowned, corpses lay everywhere, and blood flowed like rivers. Some swam away, and others scattered and fled into the fields. All sorts of chaotic situations were endless. Until about 4 p.m., after a total of six hours of pursuit, only seven bandit boats escaped (one more was later intercepted by the water police patrol in Weiting). On the hostage side, a small number were killed by stray bullets. It was also heard that the bandit leader Xie Laoyue had also been killed. As for Mao Zilong and others, after the battle of Weijingtang, they had already taken the looted precious gold, silver, foreign currency, and ornaments and fled to Shanghai in advance. That night, Camp Commander Kuang and others used steamships to tow back the captured bandits, bandit boats, bandit weapons, and rescued hostages, returning in triumph.

▲Overview of the Search for Remaining Bandits The day after the great battle of Weijingtang (i.e., during the fierce battle of Lianhua Dou on the 12th), more than ten bandit boats were also discovered on the Yangcheng Lake near Wushenjing, two or three miles away. The 11th Water Public Security Patrol continued to pursue them. The bandits did not have time to disembark and swam away. Afterwards, the 9th Public Security Watch Post of Wushenjing searched Shen Dianqiao and found a suspect named Zhang Jinru. A handkerchief, a wallet containing seventeen yuan in silver and 1,480 copper coins, and a pair of gold-plated earrings were found on his person. According to his confession, he was 26 years old, a native of Wujiang, who had been fishing for a living. On the twelfth day of the second lunar month of this year, while fishing in Hongqiao Port, he was captured by bandits and forced to row boats for them. There were three others who were captured at the same time, and the other two had already escaped. He was transferred by the Lumulu 8th Public Security Bureau to the County Bureau for interrogation. At that time, the Mu Public Security Bureau dispatched to search and arrest in four places. Two bandits were captured at Xinglong Bridge. Nine yuan in silver were found on one, and eight yuan on the other. After being brought to the bureau, one confessed that his name was Guo Wenming, 24 years old, a native of Suqian, a farmer, who came from Kunshan to Suzhou and got lost. The other, named Zhang Shoucheng, 35 years old, a native of Qingjiang, a farmer, came from Shanghai. The rest of their words were evasive, and neither admitted to being a fugitive bandit. Also, the Lumulu Security Corps squad leader searched a bandit at Nanqiao, wearing a foreign yarn short shirt inside and a velvet rope vest outside, his whole body was wet, and he had no long clothes. He confessed that his name was Qi Wenkui, 25 years old, a native of Suqian, who made a living by pulling carts and came from Shanghai. He also did not admit to being a fugitive bandit. He was sent to the 8th Bureau and transferred to the County Bureau for detention pending interrogation. Also, the Chenmu 13th Public Security Bureau reported to the county government today (14th) that they had found two abandoned bandit rifles, both stamped with the imprint of Maoqiao, Jinshan County, and 206 bullets, and 25 lead bullets from Tianmen. As for the bandits intercepted by the Youjing County Police 3rd Squad 1st Team the day before, one was named Miao Zhichuan (24 years old, a native of Haizhou), one was named Xu Magao (37 years old, a native of Huai'an), and one was named Liu Jinbiao (35 years old, a native of Suqian). They also rescued four hostages: one was named Yuan Yangru (40 years old, a native of Taiping Bridge), one was named Ni Xiaoshan (33 years old, a native of Wujiang), one was named Pang Ashou (38 years old, a native of Qingpu), and one was named Yan Ashui (27 years old, a native of Zhujiajiao). The team's firefight lasted for more than five hours, consuming a total of 1,585 bullets. Also, a wounded bandit named Gao Zi'an, 26 years old, a native of Huaiyin, was found inside the Weiting Mountain Cave by the 9th Public Security Bureau. According to the guerrilla team's verification, the bandit's real name was Zhang Shaohua, the leader of the Haizhou gang and a subordinate of the bandit leader Mao Zilong. The previous team leader, Li Guobin, was shot and killed by this bandit, but this has not yet been confirmed. Furthermore, the county government reported today, based on a report from Wu Bozhen, the 8th District Chief of Nanbeiqiao, that the Hexing steamboat, which operates from Shanghai and was going to Shanghai for boat inspection, departed from Wuxi and, while passing through Caoge Dawanli, was suddenly encountered by seventeen bandit boats that opened fire in an attempt to rob it. Fortunately, the captain of the boat managed to escape. Afterwards, it encountered a cargo ship from Shanghai and entrusted it to report to Dangkou and Huangdai to set up a blockade. Meanwhile, District Chief Wu, after receiving the news, also ordered the Li Security Corps to join the land and water police to investigate the bandits' whereabouts in the Nanqiao area. At the same time, the county government also received a report from Zhou Zhaolin, the 7th District Chief of Xiangcheng, that the sound of gunfire was very intense in Youjing yesterday afternoon around 1 p.m. It was later learned that the 2nd Battalion of the 25th Regiment had dispatched a team to join the 12th Kunshan Water Police Team and the 13th Changshu Team, as well as four warships, to continue searching for and suppressing fugitive bandits in Xizhu Village, Lianhua Dou, and other places. The firing continued until about 4 p.m., when the remaining bandits, unable to withstand the pressure, had fled towards Maota.

Another dispatch stated that in the battle of Xintian Lianhua Dou, more than eighty bandits were killed, thirty-four hostages were rescued, five bandits were captured, thirteen bandit boats were sunk, seven Mauser pistols and more than ten rifles were seized. The Haizhou gang led by Zhang Zhaohua has been almost completely wiped out. The bandit leader Zhang Zhaohua had no choice but to abandon everything, take gold and silver ornaments, and flee far away. However, Mao Zilong's unit is still taking the opportunity to steal in the Taihu area. It is said that the Pudong gang has also scattered and fled. Commander Hu has ordered the anti-bandit military police to fiercely suppress the long-standing bandits in various villages, achieving great victories. There are no large gangs of bandits left in the territories of Wuxian, Kunshan, and Wujiang counties. Only small groups of lake bandits remain, wandering aimlessly, with their roots not completely eradicated. Today, he specially ordered the county magistrates of the three counties to lead the Public Security Bureau and district chiefs to implement joint defense, conduct strict searches, and maintain public order in accordance with the anti-bandit plan.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Convening a Price Stabilization Meeting The county government convened a price stabilization meeting on the afternoon of the 14th. More than 20 people, including district chiefs and representatives from various organizations, attended. Regarding the issue of price stabilization, after discussion, it was resolved to first establish a price stabilization committee, with Zhou Heyun, Cai Zhongyu, Zhang Shengshan, Zhong Taichi, Yuan Chunlin, Zhang Yande, and Zhang Shizhi as members, to prepare and proceed. It was decided to start operations from April 22nd for two months, purchasing high-quality rice at a flat price of two yuan per stone. 72,000 yuan will be allocated from the grain reserve funds for application. Price stabilization sub-bureaus will be set up in various districts, with transportation and miscellaneous expenses borne by each district. However, the allocation of grain reserve funds requires the county to submit a request to the province for instructions. Change of Director of the County Agricultural Field The director of the County Agricultural Field, Mao Yingkui, has now been transferred to serve as the director of the Provincial Rice Trial Field by order of the provincial government. The vacant position of director of the Agricultural Field will be succeeded by Yu Yingsen. He assumed office in Datang on the day of the announcement, and the county government dispatched Pan Yongqiang, director of the Public Security Bureau, to supervise the handover nearby to ensure solemnity.

Wuxi

Guangqin Yarn Factory Holds Price Stabilization Sale Since the beginning of spring, rice prices in this county have been soaring, with the recent price of high-quality white rice reaching 16.6 yuan per stone, causing great panic among the common people. Yang Hanxi, the general manager of the Guangqin Yarn Factory in Guangqin District, and Zai Shengfu, the chief manager, considering the high rice prices and the difficult livelihoods of the workers, decided to raise a large sum of money from the factory to purchase a large quantity of white rice for sale at a flat price to benefit the workers. It is heard that the method is that every worker in the factory is allowed to buy seven he of white rice per day at 80% of the market price, for a period of two months. It is also heard that nearby factories such as Yukang Qingfeng will also do the same to maintain the livelihood of their workers.

Organizing the Scenery of Huishan The County Magistrate Sun of Wuxi has been making great efforts to organize the famous historical sites in the county. Recently, Sun plans to organize the scenery of Huishan and has specially ordered the Engineering Section of the Municipal Preparation Office to formulate a plan first and submit it to the office meeting for discussion so that it can be implemented. Yesterday, it was learned that the Engineering Section of the Municipal Office has drafted the organization plan and will submit it to the county political meeting for discussion within the day, and then submit this organization plan to the County Construction Bureau for implementation separately.

Changzhou

Caoling Port Dredging Meeting The excavation of Caoling Port in Wu County has recently been greatly impacted by continuous heavy rains and rising river water. A special emergency meeting of the river works committee was convened on the 13th at the Construction Bureau, presided over by Du Ruzhen, who reported the reasons for the meeting and the details of income and expenditure, and then discussed the cases: (1) In view of the recent heavy thunder and rain and rising river water, how should efforts be continued to advance the project? It was resolved to continue the excavation, and in terms of economics, to proceed on both sides of opening up sources and reducing expenditures. (2) The bureau's funds are running out, how should expenditures be reduced? It was resolved that all employees of the bureau would work as volunteers starting from April 16th, all supervisors would be laid off, and supervisory matters would be handled concurrently by various employees in the bureau. The administrative department would retain one person at its discretion, the secretary of the standing committee would be laid off, and the bureau's messengers would be retained at two. The engineering department's staff would be retained. (3) How to open up sources of funding in the event of insufficient funds? It was resolved to widely solicit donations. (4) What is the direction of the river project? It was resolved to re-drain the southern section, and all the mud workers in the northern section would be transferred to the southern section to help with the digging.

Suicide Case at the Ji'an Inn There was a woman and a sick man staying in room number six at the Ji'an Inn in Banshanting, Wu County, on the evening of the 12th. Unexpectedly, the man died that night. On the 13th, it was rumored in society as a strange event. Later, a suicide note was found next to the deceased, and it was learned that the deceased's name was Mei Caibao, from Ningbo, 26 years old, working as a fireman on a Yong'an steamboat. He was in conflict with Wang Aju, a woman also working on the boat, and his position was unstable. He was also suffering from syphilis and was in great pain, so he committed suicide. The woman is his mistress, named Yi Guoying. How he committed suicide is still unclear. The Public Security Bureau has dispatched inspector Pu Zhengshu to investigate and will report it to the county court to send someone for an autopsy.

Jiangyin

Taixing Bandit Captured in Cheng Xu Jinwen's family in Dujiazhuang, Taixing 2nd District, was robbed last autumn, and the ringleader Zhang Shaoqing shot and killed the owner. Xu Jinwen's son, Xu Huangming, inquired and learned that the bandit was hiding in Jiang County at the beginning of this month. He immediately presented a document to the Taixing County Government to consult with the Jiang County Government to capture him. The day before yesterday (13th), Xu took his informant in person and successfully arrested him in a house opposite the Fuchang Renji Dyeing Workshop outside the North Gate and detained him in the Public Security Bureau Detention Center, waiting for Taixing to send police to bring him back for interrogation. Financial Inspector Came to Cheng to Investigate Finance The Financial Inspector Wang Junsun came to Cheng the night before last (12th) to investigate the case of the former Finance Bureau Director Dai colluding to speculate, and to investigate the transfer of the Farmers Bank Fund. It is heard that the investigation of the collusion and speculation involved an investigation by the current Finance Bureau Director Shen Lunxu to determine whether the speculation was disassociated from the fund. As a result, the former Director Dai was found to have violated the order to speculate. It is proposed to petition the provincial government for punishment. He left Cheng yesterday.

Rugao

Meeting on City Defense Measures In view of the recent unrest in the area and the spread of rumors, the county government specially convened a meeting of military police and various agencies at the government on the morning of the 10th to discuss city defense measures. It was decided to organize a city defense committee to unify the command of the military police. The details were not announced because they involved military secrets. The county government also announced a special curfew starting today. The city gates will be opened at 6 a.m. and closed at 8 p.m. Traffic will be cut off at 10 p.m., and no passage will be allowed without a password.

Communist Bandits Plot to Attack Longju Harbor The Communist bandits in the southern countryside of Juegang District, after being fiercely suppressed by government troops for days, suffered heavy losses. Unexpectedly, they recently sent someone to contact the sea bandits and agreed to meet at the Sangan Port north of the Jiumen Gate to plot to attack Longju Harbor. The city is now under strict defense.

Wang Jinqiu Kidnapped for Ransom Wang Jinqiu, an employee of Rentai Warehouse, located outside the dike of Juegang near the Jiumen Gate, was suddenly kidnapped by more than 20 bandits on the night of the 5th. On the 7th, the bandits sent a letter demanding a ransom of 4,000 yuan.

Nantong

Military Police Bust Bandit Den The commander of Liu Camp of the 5th Division stationed in Shanghai, together with the 13th Company of the Provincial Police Force, suppressed bandits in the Yu Xi Yuan area on the 12th. They busted an organization in a tea garden in Beixing Bridge. The bandits opened fire and resisted arrest. Three people were killed, eight key criminals were arrested, and many documents were seized. They were escorted to the city for interrogation.

Rice Shortage Causes Panic in Tongcheng Nantong's source of rice has been cut off. The current rice reserves are only more than 14,000 shi. Panic has broken out in the market. The price is 25.4 yuan per shi. Representatives from all walks of life have resolved to rush to buy Annam rice for flat price sales to provide relief.

Provincial Task Force Goes to Juegang to Suppress Sea Bandits More than 30 bandit boats suddenly arrived in the waters off Juegang. Sea bandits landed and harassed the area. The Provincial Police Force stationed in the city sent a hand-held machine gun squad and a tracking artillery team to suppress them. According to telephone news on the evening of the 13th, the police and bandits came into contact at noon. The bandits retreated to the sea in four directions.

Meeting on Post-Suppression Measures in East Village Representatives from various party, government, military, and police agencies in Nantong jointly discussed post-suppression measures in East Village. Chen Bu, Liu, and others were designated to discuss search methods for lurking bandits, conduct thorough rural cleanup, and concentrate security regiments and police teams in various bandit areas to strengthen defenses.

Zhenjiang

Police Brigade Captures Kidnappers Xu Guozhi, a member of the 3rd Squad of the Police Brigade stationed in Huangxu, together with Jiang Jiaqi, a sectional railway police officer, and Qu Changqing, a squad member, captured the kidnapper Yuan Zhai at the Xinfeng Station at around 7 p.m. yesterday when the 17th slow train arrived. Later, they captured three kidnappers, Shao Alin, Zhu Qingbo, and others, on the South Platform. Two Brownings were found on Shao and Zhu. They were taken back by the military police stationed at Xinfeng Station and sent to the Provincial Military Police Battalion Headquarters for interrogation.

National Goods Exhibition Opens Today The Provincial National Goods Exhibition will be held at 2 p.m. today (15th) at the Public Lecture Hall of Bo Xian Park. The exhibition hall is located at the Jiangbian Yidu Pier. The exhibition hours are from 9 a.m. to 8 p.m. There are more than 10,000 kinds of fine national goods participating. The association has invited people from all walks of life to attend the opening ceremony. In addition to speeches, an entertainment party will be held in the lecture hall in the evening.

Funing

Bandit Shi Yicheng Arrested Shi Yicheng, a well-known bandit in Lianfu County, nicknamed "Stone Big Nose," kidnapped Liu Yuchuan's niece and Zuo Zan's daughter the day before yesterday and fled without a trace. After Liu Zuo reported the case, Huang Gongzheng, the captain of the police team, arrested the bandit Shi and sent him to the team headquarters. He was transferred to the county government for interrogation today (11th).

Election of District Party Committee Members The Funing County Party Headquarters, First District Party Headquarters, convened a general meeting of party members in the district yesterday to elect the third executive committee. As a result, Gu Fenglou, Qiu Yixin, and Meng Xinmin were elected as executive committee members, and Gu Baosong and Dai Bingwu were elected as alternate executive committee members. Gu Fenglou was elected as the standing committee member, Qiu Yixin was elected as the organization and training committee member, and Meng Xinmin was elected as the propaganda committee member.

Gaoyou

Bandits Burn and Loot Cangtie Village Several bandit boats carrying thirty or forty bandits suddenly docked at Cangtie Village in the county on the evening of the day before yesterday. Each of them held guns and scattered sentries ashore. The residents fled in droves. At 9 p.m., the bandits held weapons and searched house by house, looting fifteen families in a row and setting fire to more than thirty families, causing losses of about 50,000 to 60,000 yuan.

Taizhou

Details of Bandit Suppression It has been reported that in recent days, more than a thousand bandits have gathered in Tiantai, Beishan, Tongbai Palace, and other places, wearing Zhejiang Red Army symbols on their chests. The situation is very rampant. Wang Delong, the camp commander of the 1st Battalion of the 5th Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Government Security Team stationed in Ninghai, learned of this and immediately led two companies of troops to suppress them. After three days and nights of attack, the bandits could not hold out and fled to Xinchang. It is estimated that dozens of bandits were killed, dozens of guns, one cannon, and two flags were seized.

Large Fire on Dongsheng Street A fire suddenly broke out at Songyunge Paper Store on Haimen Sheng Street, Linhai, the day before yesterday. In an instant, the fire blazed into the sky and could not be extinguished. The fire brigade rushed to the scene and tried their best to put it out. It was extinguished after about an hour. It is estimated that more than thirty stores were burned down, causing losses of about 100,000 yuan.

Jiaxing

Business Wheel Freight and Passenger Account Donation Determined by the Company The inland small business wheels operating in Jiaxing last month received a provincial order forwarded by the county magistrate to collect a passenger and freight donation of 10%, which has been collected with the bureau's ticket, and forwarded to the county for transfer to the province for use. Now, each wheel company feels that it is too much trouble to collect by ticket, and that adding 10% to passenger tickets is also a major obstacle to the economy of passengers. Therefore, Yongji, China Merchants, and other ten wheel companies have proposed to pay a total of 200 yuan per month for passenger and freight account donations, and the passenger and freight tickets will also be increased by 2, 3, or 4 cents each, in order to facilitate the operation and relieve business difficulties. They have jointly written a letter to the Chamber of Commerce to forward it to the county government for approval. It is now learned that the Finance Bureau of the County Government feels that 200 yuan per month seems too little. A meeting of managers of each wheel bureau was specially convened a few days ago. As a result, each bureau recognized a total of 250 yuan per month as account donations. The county has now prepared a table of account donations collected by each wheel bureau and submitted it to the province for approval.

Huzhou

Bandits Intercept Night Boats Three night boats from Kunji, Miao Ji, Hong Ji, etc., which departed from Sian to Huzhou, were intercepted by bandits who spoke with a Yu accent on the afternoon of the 11th, passing through the junction of Niudian Bridge and Tangkou. At that time, it was already late at night. Suddenly, seven bandits were seen on the shore, firing a shot and shouting to stop. Each boat stopped upon hearing the sound. One bandit held a white Brownin on the shore as a lookout. The remaining six unarmed bandits each held a flashlight and arbitrarily searched each boat, robbing the passengers of all their clothes and silver, and the boatmen of the rice they were carrying. They went west. And Hong Ji's boat had already been completely robbed of its cargo by several bandits halfway from Huzhou to Si'an the day before. Unfortunately, it was robbed again on its return trip to Huzhou the next day.

Headquarters Executes Two Bandits The famous long-term bandit Shen Ashou and the key criminal Zhang Shilin, who privately transported guns for the bandits, were arrested. After interrogation by the Military Law Office of the Headquarters, the bandits confessed without reservation. Therefore, at around 5 p.m. yesterday, the headquarters verified the identities of the two criminals, escorted them to the South School Ground, and executed them by shooting.

Shaoxing

Cao'e River to Be Dredged The Cao'e River has a total area of 13,000 square li. The riverbed is silted up. Zhang Jingxu, the county magistrate of Shangyu, has formulated a plan and submitted it to the Construction Conference for approval. The Construction Department has submitted it to the department for detailed discussion. It is said that the required funds will be allocated from the Construction Public Bonds.

Mingguang

Security Corps Busts Kidnappers The youngest son of Chen Xiantang of Chen Wanshun Silk Fabric Store in Nantao, this town, was kidnapped on the 22nd of last month by his servant Cai San and other bandits. At that time, investigations were carried out everywhere, but there was no trace. After the Security Corps learned that the bandits were hiding in Shangzhu Village, more than seventy li north of Mingguang, Captain Zhou led a team in the rain last night (11th) to rescue the hostage. He also captured two bandits, Zhu Wantang and Zhu Wanjun, on the spot, and brought them back for interrogation. The criminals confessed to being bandits and were immediately sent to the county for prosecution.

National Education Conference Opens Today

Opening ceremony to be held in Beijing this afternoon

Chairman Chiang to attend and deliver a speech

The Second National Education Conference will open in the capital today. Discussions will begin tomorrow and continue until the 22nd. The Education Administration Conference will be held continuously. The news received yesterday is recorded below.

Preparation Process

The preparation process of the Ministry of Education for the Second National Education Conference is recorded below.

(I) Origin

(I) Since the Third National Congress of the Kuomintang of the Republic of China decided on the educational purpose of the Republic of China: "The education of the Republic of China is based on the Three Principles of the People, with the aim of enriching people's lives, supporting the survival of society, developing the national economy, and continuing the life of the nation, striving for national independence, universal civil rights, and development of people's livelihood, so as to promote universal harmony." After the Second Plenary Session of the Central Committee resolved to have the Ministry of Education convene a National Education Conference in the spring of the 19th year of the Republic of China to discuss the education plan organized by the Ministry of Education and the various education plans compiled by the Compilation Committee, the nature of this National Education Conference, although slightly different from the first National Education Conference convened by the University Council the year before, which was conducted automatically and with free proposals from attending members, the purpose of pooling wisdom and solving important educational problems is the same.

(II) On January 24th of the 19th year of the Republic of China, the Ministry of Education organized a preparatory committee for the National Education Conference to be fully responsible for all preparatory matters, and appointed one chairman and one vice-chairman, and twelve members, with five executive committee members. Its organization was divided into five sections: document, editing, accounting, general affairs, and reception. Each section had one director, concurrently held by a committee member, and several staff members, concurrently filled by officials from the Ministry of Education.

(II) First Standing Committee Meeting

The main items decided at the First Standing Committee Meeting (February 7th, 19th year) were: (I) The accounting section should refer to the seven receipts and expenditures to prepare a budget and submit it to the meeting for decision; (II) Discuss the main points of the National Education Conference Regulations, and discuss them item by item based on the regulations of the First Education Conference. The main points are as follows: (I) Qualifications for membership: 1. The Director of the Provincial Department of Education or their representative, one person per province; 2. The Provincial Department of Education designates the Director of the Education Bureau of each province, city, or county, one person per province; 3. The Director of the Education Bureau of the Special Municipality or their representative, one person per city; 4. The President of the National University or their representative, one person per university; 5. Twenty-four experts, one person per field; 6. Minister, Vice-Minister, Counselor, and Director of the Ministry of Education; (II) The Minister of Education will be the speaker, and two additional vice-speakers will be set up, one appointed by the Vice-Minister of Political Affairs of the Ministry of Education, and one elected by the General Assembly; (III) The meeting date is tentatively set for April 15th to 22nd; (IV) The Minister and Deputy Minister of the Central Training Department are invited to attend the meeting for guidance; (V) Expert members will be given travel expenses as appropriate, and the rest will be borne by the respective agencies, but the conference will provide accommodation and meals; (III) Discuss the methods for receiving members: (I) In Shanghai, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau is requested to be responsible for the reception, and the guest house of the Shanghai Commercial and Chinese Bank is provided; (II) In Nanjing, the reception section staff will receive guests at the station and wharf, and the Nanjing Municipal Education Bureau will be asked to send two bureau members to assist in the reception; (III) Rent rooms in the Central Hotel or other hotels as dormitories for staff members; (IV) Discuss the selection of staff members of the committee. The directors of each section will first nominate five people, and after consultation, ask the minister to appoint them; (V) Discuss the agenda of the first meeting of the committee on the 10th of this month: 1. Chairman's report, 2. Discuss the draft regulations of the National Education Conference, 3. Discuss the budget of the National Education Conference, 4. Discuss the methods for receiving members, 5. Nominate staff members for each section of the committee, 6. Other.

(III) First Preparatory Meeting

Main items decided at the First Preparatory Meeting (2:00 PM on February 10th, 19th year): (I) National Education Conference Regulations (Ministry Order promulgated on February 14th, 19th year); (II) National Education Conference Budget; (III) Methods for Receiving Members; (IV) Nomination of Staff Members for Each Section; (V) Add one famous person's speech at the National Education Conference.

The first preparatory meeting decided on the budget for the National Education Conference: (I) Accommodation and food expenses, revised to 6,150 yuan; (II) Tour fee, revised to 1,500 yuan; (III) Travel expenses, revised to 3,000 yuan; (IV) Postage and telegraph, revised to 500 yuan; (V) Purchase, revised to 500 yuan; (VI) Consumption, revised to 300 yuan; (VII) Advertising, revised to 300 yuan. The total budget is 18,450 yuan.

(IV) Second Standing Committee Meeting

Main items decided at the Third Standing Committee Meeting (10:00 AM on March 13th, 19th year): (I) Regarding the general affairs section: (I) The venue for the entire event will be the auditorium of the Ministry of Railways; (II) Members' dormitory will be rented at the Central Hotel; (III) The badge will have a circular shape with the four characters "Psychological Construction" engraved in the middle; (IV) Each section may use wooden stands; (II) Regarding the Head of the Reception Section: (I) Contact various agencies to arrange the reception of members; (II) Add female staff members from the ministry to serve as staff members of the reception section; (III) Regarding the document section: (I) The rules of procedure should stipulate: A. Discussion of motions does not require voting procedures. If members have two or more opinions on the same motion, they may be forwarded to the audit department for decision. B. The group review meeting may invite specialist committee members of the case preparation committee or the section chiefs in charge of the Ministry of Education to attend; (II) Temporary clerks will not be employed for the time being, and will be considered when necessary; (III) Two stenographers, each with a salary of 50 yuan; (IV) The meeting recorder is temporarily set at four people: Gao Weichang, Wang Fengbai, Gu Liangjie, and Xu Xudong; (IV) Regarding the editor: (I) The conference handbook should be revised based on the one printed in the previous session; (II) The meeting schedule is set as review in the morning and general assembly in the afternoon; (III) The agenda for the first day is: 1. Draw lots for member seating, 2. Discuss the rules of procedure, 3. Discuss the rules of the group review, 4. Elect the vice-speaker, 5. Nominate the reviewers, 6. Opening of the meeting; (V) Regarding the opening ceremony, the people invited to attend the meeting are decided as follows: (I) Chairman of the National Government; (II) Presidents and Vice-Presidents of the Five Yuan; (III) Central Party Headquarters, Presidents, Vice-Presidents, and Secretaries-General of the Three Ministries; (IV) Central Executive Committee; (V) Party Headquarters of the Capital City; (VI) Central Political School; (VII) Ministers of Various Ministries, Chairmen of Various Committees, Mayor of the Capital City, President of the Supreme Court, and Chief of General Staff; (VI) Add staff members to each section.

(V) Third Standing Committee Meeting

Third Standing Committee Meeting, (2:00 PM on February 25th, 19th year), (I) Draft the meeting schedule: Opening at 2:00 PM on April 15th, general assembly opens at 9:00 AM on the 16th, review meeting in the afternoon, review meeting on the 17th in the morning, general assembly in the afternoon, review meeting on the 18th in the morning, general assembly in the afternoon, review meeting on the 19th in the morning, general assembly in the afternoon, review meeting on the 21st in the morning, general assembly in the afternoon, general assembly in the morning on the 22nd, closing in the afternoon, (III) The rules for spectators will be modified according to the previous regulations.

Conference Chairman Jiang Menglin

For future use (III) Regarding the work reports or publications of various agencies, those distributed to each member should be handed over to the reception section for distribution (IV) The issue of travel expenses for expert committee members, (V) Zheng Tianting and Zhao Qian will be responsible for the daily newspaper editing (VI) Maps will be distributed to each member, one for each person, handled by the general affairs section (VII) The next preparatory committee meeting will be held at 2:00 PM on April 12th (VIII) The location of the review meeting will be temporarily determined according to the situation, and the meetings will be held in groups at the Ministry of Education or the Central Hotel (IX) The issue of using cars during the meeting (X) The car rules will be drafted by the reception section (XI) The name of the manual will be "Second National Education Conference Handbook," with the conference emblem printed on the cover (XII) A silver wreath will be presented to the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum, handled by the general affairs section, with a value limited to 300 yuan.

(VI) Second Preparatory Meeting

Second Preparatory Meeting (2:00 PM on April 12th) Committee members present: Chen Jianxiu, Zhu Baoqin, Jiang Shaomo, Zheng Tianting, Gu Shusen, Dai Chao, Zhao Naichuan, Zhu Jingnong, Chairman Zhu Jingnong, Recorder Zhou Gan. (I) Meeting as scheduled, (II) Reading of the minutes of the last meeting and the minutes of the previous standing committee meetings, (III) Reports from each section on the work situation, Chairman's report, and Chairman asked Committee Member Chen Jianxiu to act as chairman due to important matters, (IV) Discussion of the draft rules of procedure for the general assembly, which were revised and passed item by item, (V) Discussion of the draft review rules for the general assembly, which were revised and passed item by item, (VI) Discussion of the articles of association for the daily newspaper of the general assembly, which were revised and passed item by item, and the meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

In addition, matters decided at the Second Preparatory Standing Committee Meeting (I) Contact news reporters, Guo Youshou is the general contact, Zhang Banghua is the contact at the ministry, and Guo Yunfeng is the contact at the meeting; (II) Reception of members, Zhu Shusen, the general receiver, entertains at the Central Hotel.

Expediting Review of Proposals

The National Education Conference opens today. The Plan for Improving National Education drafted by the Education Plan Preparation Committee has been sent to the Central Political Conference for review. The Central Political Conference handed it over to the Education Group for review, and the review meeting was convened by Committee Member Dai Jitao. Later, because most of the members of the Education Group went to Hangzhou to participate in the National Games and did not return, the Secretariat of the Central Political Conference sent personnel to Hangzhou with the plan to ask the members for their opinions. Now, because the National Education Conference opens today, the plan urgently needs to be reviewed so that it can be discussed. It is reported that the Secretariat of the Central Political Conference urgently telegraphed Huzhou, Hangzhou, and other places to urge Committee Member Dai and others to return to the capital.

Chairman Jiang to Attend and Deliver a Speech

Nanjing Telegram: Chairman Jiang plans to attend the National Education Conference on the 15th and deliver a speech.

Party and state dignitaries are required to attend today's opening ceremony. Because this morning is the regular meeting of the Executive Yuan, the opening ceremony of the conference has been moved to 2:00 PM to allow all dignitaries to attend. It is reported that Chairman Jiang has notified the conference that he will be allowed to attend the ceremony, and all the heads of the Yuan, ministers, and central committee members will attend. Li Shizeng and Wu Zhihui arrived in the capital on the 13th and reported to the conference. Cai Yuanpei telegraphed the Ministry of Education, saying that he would leave Shanghai on the night train on the 15th and come to the capital. Minister Jiang has urgently telegraphed Cai to ask him to come to the capital on the night train on the 14th.

Various Aspects of the Conference

▲Changes in Membership

Nanjing Telegram: Expert Tao Xingzhi is unable to attend due to matters, and the conference has re-hired Yu Zheng as an education expert to fill the vacancy of Tao. Huang Jianzhong, Director of the Higher Education Department of the Ministry of Education, has been transferred to Director of the Hubei Education Bureau. The Ministry of Education has reassigned Xie Shuying, Chief of the First Section of the department, to represent the Higher Education Department, and Ku Qijun, Chief of the Section of Mongolian and Tibetan Education, to represent the Mongolian and Tibetan Department.

▲Adding a Conference Venue Secretary

Guo Youshou

Nanjing Telegram: The conference venue secretaries were previously appointed as Wu Yan Yin and Zhong

Xiu. Because the conference venue affairs are heavy, and the two people may not be enough to handle it, Guo Youshou, Chief of the Higher Education Department of the Ministry of Education, has been specially hired to be the conference venue secretary. ▲Design of the Conference Badge

The conference badge is divided into two types: A silver-made round badge with white characters and a blue background, with the four characters "Psychological Construction" engraved in seal script in the middle. The design is as shown on the left. Each member and staff member will be issued one. The number is marked on the back for confidential examination. In addition, each person wears a ribbon badge, with the Party emblem printed on the top, and the nine characters "Second National Education Conference" printed in the middle. The name of the member is written on the left side of the characters. However, the member badge is white, the staff badge is light blue, and the guest badge is purple, to distinguish them. The design is the same for all. The square seal of the Second National Education Conference is stamped below the badge to prevent counterfeiting. ▲Central University to be responsible for members' medical care

Nanjing Telegram: The medical care of the conference members has been arranged by the reception section with the Central Hospital. The regulations are as follows: (I) All members of this conference can go to the Central Hospital for diagnosis and treatment; (II) Members seeking medical treatment must present their badge or official letter from this conference as proof; (III) When seeking medical treatment, they must pay the regular registration fee at the registration desk (10 cents for the first visit and 10 copper coins for a follow-up visit). The diagnosis fee will be borne by this conference, but the treatment will be given according to special registration, and treatment will be given as soon as they arrive; (IV) The diagnosis and treatment time is from 1:30 PM to 4:00 PM every day; (V) In case of serious illness, the reception desk can telegraph the Central Hospital to send an ambulance.
